                            $('#myForm').validator().on('submit', function (e) {
                                if (e.isDefaultPrevented()) {
                                    // handle the invalid form...
                                    return false;
                                } else {
                                    // everything looks good!
                                    return register_stick_stu('myForm');
                                }
                                return false;
                            })
                            $('#myForm_login').validator().on('submit', function (e) {
                                if (e.isDefaultPrevented()) {
                                    return false;
                                } else {
                                    return login_stick_stu('myForm_login');
                                }
                                return false;
                            })
                            $('#myForm_forgot').validator().on('submit', function (e) {
                                if (e.isDefaultPrevented()) {
                                    return false;
                                } else {
                                    return send_password_stick_stu('myForm_forgot');
                                }
                                return false;
                            })
                            function toggle_form(id) {
                                $(".toggle").hide();
                                $("#" + id).show();
                            }
                            function register_stick_stu(form_id) {
                                $('#screen').css({"display": "block"});
                                var type_d = $("#modal-title-reg").html();
                                var type_val = 'Shortlist_stick';
                                var open_link;
                                if (type_d.indexOf('View Phone Number') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'Phone_Info';
                                }
                                else if (type_d.indexOf('Phone') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'Phone';
                                }
                                else if (type_d.indexOf('Register to Vote up this Review') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'Voteup';
                                }
                                else if (type_d.indexOf('Email') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'Email';
                                }
                                else if (type_d.indexOf('Download') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'Download';
                                }
                                else if (type_d.indexOf('Get Contact Info') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'Contact_Info';
                                }
                                else if (type_d.indexOf('Get Updates') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'GetUpdate';
                                }
                                else if (type_d.indexOf('College Search') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'CollegeSearch';
                                }
                                else if (type_d.indexOf('Know More') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'knowmore';
                                    open_link = $("#modal-link").html();
                                }

                                //storeInfo(type_val + 'new');
                                var x = document.getElementById(form_id);
                                var form_value = {};
                                var i;
                                for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
                                    if (x.elements[i].name == 'db_access' || x.elements[i].name == 'studyAborad') {
                                        if (document.getElementById("db_access").checked == true) {
                                            form_value['db_access'] = 'Y';
                                        } else {
                                            form_value['db_access'] = 'N';
                                        }
                                        if (document.getElementById("studyAborad").checked == true) {
                                            form_value['studyAborad'] = 'Y';
                                        } else {
                                            form_value['studyAborad'] = 'N';
                                        }
                                    }
                                    else {
                                        form_value[x.elements[i].name] = x.elements[i].value;
                                    }
                                }
                                form_value['pages'] = "/colleges/national-school-of-business-nsb-bangalore$institute_profile" + "_" + type_val;
                                delete form_value['already_reg'];
                                var full_path = "https://www.collegesearch.in";
                                var main_url = full_path + "/ajax/student_registration.php";
                                $.ajax({type: "GET", url: main_url, async: false, data: form_value, success: function (response) {
                                        if (response.search("Register Successful") != -1) {
                                            if (type_val == 'Phone') {
                                                storeInfo(type_val + 'save');
                                                window.location.reload();
                                            }
                                            else if (type_val == 'Email') {
                                                storeInfo(type_val + 'save');
                                                window.location.reload();
                                            }
                                            else if (type_val == 'Download') {
                                                storeInfo(type_val + 'save');
                                                window.location.reload();
                                            }
                                            else if (type_val == 'Voteup') {
                                                alreadyLogged = 1;
                                                $('#myModal').modal('hide');
                                                $('#screen').css({"display": "none"});
                                                VoteUp();
                                                return false;

                                            }
                                            else if (type_val == 'Contact_Info') {
                                                storeInfo(type_val + 'Contact');
                                                window.open("https://www.collegesearch.in/colleges/national-school-of-business-nsb-bangalore/contact", "_self");
                                            }
                                            else if (type_val == 'Phone_Info') {
                                                storeInfo(type_val + 'Contact');
                                                //alert('Thank You for sharing the details! College will contact you soon!');
                                                window.open("https://www.collegesearch.in/colleges/national-school-of-business-nsb-bangalore/contact", "_self");
                                            }
                                            else if (type_val == 'GetUpdate') {
                                                exam_follow();
                                                storeInfo(type_val + 'GetUpdate');
                                                window.location.reload();
                                            }
                                            else if (type_val == 'knowmore') {
                                                var win = window.open(open_link, '_blank');
                                                storeInfo(type_val + '_barter');
                                                window.location.reload();
                                                win.focus();
                                            }
                                            else if (type_val == 'CollegeSearch') {
                                                storeInfo(type_val + 'CollegeSearch');
                                                window.location.reload();
                                            }
                                            else {
                                                addToShortList();
                                                storeInfo(type_val + 'Shortlist_stick');
                                                $('.select_shortlist').hide();
                                                window.location.reload();
                                            }
                                        }
                                        else {
                                            $('#screen').css({"display": "none"});
                                            alert('This Email ID already Exists. Please Login!');
                                            return false;
                                        }
                                    },
                                    error: function () {
                                        $('#screen').css({"display": "none"});
                                        return false;
                                    }
                                });
                                return false;
                            }
                            function checkDuplicateStudent_email(email) {
                                var full_path = "https://www.collegesearch.in";
                                var main_url = full_path + "/ajax.php?action=checkDuplicateStudent&email=" + email;
                                $.ajax({type: "GET", url: main_url, async: false,
                                    success: function (response) {
                                        if (response.search('Duplicate exist') != -1) {
                                            document.getElementById('email').value = '';
                                            document.getElementById('email').focus();
                                            $("#email_check").toggleClass("has-error");
                                            $("#email_check_not").toggleClass("glyphicon-remove");
                                            alert("Entered email already exists");
                                        }
                                    }
                                });
                            }
                            function login_stick_stu(form_id) {
                                $('#screen').css({"display": "block"});
                                var type_d = $("#modal-title-reg").html();
                                var type_val = 'Shortlist_stick';
                                var open_link;

                                if (type_d.indexOf('View Phone Number') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'Phone_Info';
                                }
                                else if (type_d.indexOf('Phone') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'Phone';
                                }
                                else if (type_d.indexOf('Register to Vote up this Review') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'Voteup';
                                }
                                else if (type_d.indexOf('Email') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'Email';
                                }
                                else if (type_d.indexOf('Download') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'Download';
                                }
                                else if (type_d.indexOf('Get Contact Info') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'Contact_Info';
                                }
                                else if (type_d.indexOf('Get Updates') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'GetUpdate';
                                }
                                else if (type_d.indexOf('College Search') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'CollegeSearch';
                                }
                                else if (type_d.indexOf('Know More') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'knowmore';
                                    open_link = $("#modal-link").html();
                                }

                                //storeInfo(type_val + 'new');
                                var x = document.getElementById(form_id);
                                var form_value = {};
                                var i;
                                for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
                                    form_value[x.elements[i].name] = x.elements[i].value;
                                }
                                form_value['pages'] = "/colleges/national-school-of-business-nsb-bangalore$institute_profile" + "_" + type_val;
                                form_value['remember_student'] = 'Y';
                                var full_path = "https://www.collegesearch.in";
                                var main_url = full_path + "/ajax/student_login.php";
                                $.ajax({type: "GET", url: main_url, async: false, data: form_value, success: function (response) {
                                        if (response.search("Login Successful") != -1) {
                                            if (type_val == 'Phone') {
                                                storeInfo(type_val + 'save');
                                                window.location.reload();
                                            }
                                            else if (type_val == 'Email') {
                                                storeInfo(type_val + 'save');
                                                window.location.reload();
                                            }
                                            else if (type_val == 'Download') {
                                                storeInfo(type_val + 'save');
                                                window.location.reload();
                                            }
                                            else if (type_val == 'Contact_Info') {
                                                storeInfo(type_val + 'Contact');
                                                window.open("https://www.collegesearch.in/colleges/national-school-of-business-nsb-bangalore/contact", "_self");
                                            }
                                            else if (type_val == 'CollegeSearch') {
                                                storeInfo(type_val + 'CollegeSearch');
                                                window.location.reload();
                                            }
                                            else if (type_val == 'Voteup') {
                                                alreadyLogged = 1;
                                                $('#myModal').modal('hide');
                                                $('#screen').css({"display": "none"});
                                                VoteUp();
                                                return false;

                                            }
                                            else if (type_val == 'Phone_Info') {
                                                storeInfo(type_val + 'Contact');
                                                //alert('Thank You for sharing the details! College will contact you soon!');
                                                window.open("https://www.collegesearch.in/colleges/national-school-of-business-nsb-bangalore/contact", "_self");
                                            }
                                            else if (type_val == 'GetUpdate') {
                                                exam_follow();
                                                storeInfo(type_val + 'GetUpdate');
                                                window.location.reload();
                                            }
                                            else if (type_val == 'knowmore') {
                                                var win = window.open(open_link, '_blank');
                                                storeInfo(type_val + '_barter');
                                                window.location.reload();
                                                win.focus();
                                            }
                                            else {
                                                addToShortList();
                                                storeInfo(type_val + 'Shortlist_stick');
                                                $('.select_shortlist').hide();
                                                window.location.reload();
                                            }
                                        }
                                        else {
                                            $('#screen').css({"display": "none"});
                                            alert('Incorrect Password');
                                            return false;
                                        }
                                    },
                                    error: function () {
                                        $('#screen').css({"display": "none"});
                                        alert('Incorrect Password');
                                        return false;
                                    }
                                });
                                return false;
                            }
                            function send_password_stick_stu(form_id) {
                                var x = document.getElementById(form_id);
                                var form_value = {};
                                var i;
                                for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
                                    form_value[x.elements[i].name] = x.elements[i].value;
                                }
                                $.ajax({
                                    type: "POST",
                                    url: "https://www.collegesearch.in/ajax/ajax_forgot_password.php",
                                    data: form_value,
                                    cache: false,
                                    success: function (response)
                                    {
                                        if (response.search('success') != -1) {
                                            $("#sent_pass_error").hide();
                                            $("#sent_pass").show();
                                        } else {
                                            $("#sent_pass").hide();
                                            $("#sent_pass_error").show();
                                        }
                                    }
                                });
                                return false;
                            }

    function toggleMe(keyy) {

        return true;
    }
    function storeInfo(type) {
        var main_url = "https://www.collegesearch.in/ajax/reg-track-popup?type=" + type;
        //alert(main_url);
        $.ajax({type: "GET", url: main_url, async: false, success:
                    function () {
                        //alert('saved');
                    }
        });
    }
    $('#myModal').on('show.bs.modal', function (event) {
        var button = $(event.relatedTarget) // Button that triggered the modal
        var text = button.data('head') // Extract info from data-* attributes
        // If necessary, you could initiate an AJAX request here (and then do the updating in a callback).
        // Update the modal's content. We'll use jQuery here, but you could use a data binding library or other methods instead.
        var modal = $(this)
        if(text=='College Search'){
            modal.find('#modal-title-reg').text('Register on  ' + text)
            modal.find('#modal-title-log').text('Login on  ' + text)
        }
        else{
            modal.find('#modal-title-reg').text('Register to  ' + text)
            modal.find('#modal-title-log').text('Login to  ' + text)
        }
        if (text == 'Know More') {
            var link = button.data('whatever')
            modal.find('#modal-link').text(link)
        }
    })

    $('#myModal').on('show.bs.modal', function (event) {
        var button = $(event.relatedTarget) // Button that triggered the modal
        var text = button.data('head') // Extract info from data-* attributes
        // If necessary, you could initiate an AJAX request here (and then do the updating in a callback).
        // Update the modal's content. We'll use jQuery here, but you could use a data binding library or other methods instead.
        var modal = $(this)
        if(text=='College Search'){
            modal.find('#modal-title-reg').text('Register on  ' + text)
            modal.find('#modal-title-log').text('Login on  ' + text)
        }
        else{
            modal.find('#modal-title-reg').text('Register to  ' + text)
            modal.find('#modal-title-log').text('Login to  ' + text)
        }
        if(text == 'Know More'){
            var link = button.data('whatever')
            modal.find('#modal-link').text(link)
        }
    })

        //alert(main_url);
        $.ajax({type: "GET", url: main_url, async: false, success:
            function () {
                //alert('saved');
            }
        });
    }

    function voteUpReview(id){

    main_url_fetch = "https://www.collegesearch.in/ajax/vote-up-review-bharat.php?review_id="+id;
    $.ajax({
            type: "GET",
            url: main_url_fetch,
            async: false,
            success: function (data)
            {
                if(data.search("already") > -1) {
                    alert('You have already voted up this Review.');
                }else{
                    $('#vote_up_count_'+id).html(data);
                }
                $('#vote_up_count_'+id).css('visibility','visible');
                $('#vote_up_count_'+id).prev('.helpfullBtn').prop('onclick',null);
                $('#vote_up_count_'+id).prev('.helpfullBtn').css('cursor','text');
                $('#vote_up_count_'+id).prev('.helpfullBtn').find('i.fa.fa-thumbs-up.thumbs-up-counter').css('color','#a5c82d');

            }
        });
}

function validatePhone(phone) {var pattern2 = new RegExp(/^[0]?[789]\d{9}$/);return pattern2.test(phone);}

function sendapplink(type, page) {var phone_value = $('#app_link_phone').val();
			if (phone_value.length < 10) {
                alert('Enter Valid Phone Number');return false;
            } else {
                var phone_test = validatePhone(phone_value);
                if (phone_test) {
                    if (phone_value != '') {
                        alert('SMS sent. Happy Searching!');
                        trackLinkSend('phone', phone_value, 'MobileAppPage');
                    }
                } else {
                    alert('Enter Valid Phone Numbers');
                }
        }
    }
function trackLinkSend(type, val, page) {var main_url = "https://www.collegesearch.in/ajax/track-send-mobileapp-link?type=" + type + "&val=" + val + "&page=" + page;
        $.ajax({type: "GET", url: main_url, async: false, success: function(){}
        });
    }

function selectCourse(id, course_type){
    $('#showLoad').css({"display": "block"});$('html, body').css({'overflow': 'hidden','height': '100%'});
    var dataString = 'id=' + id + '&course_type=' + course_type;
    $.ajax({ type: "POST",url: "https://www.collegesearch.in/ajax/changeCourse.php",data: dataString,cache: false,async:true,success: function (html){ window.location.href = 'https://www.collegesearch.in/colleges/national-school-of-business-nsb-bangalore'; }});
}

                            $('#myForm').validator().on('submit', function (e) {
                                if (e.isDefaultPrevented()) {
                                    // handle the invalid form...
                                    return false;
                                } else {
                                    // everything looks good!
                                    return register_stick_stu('myForm');
                                }
                                return false;
                            })
                            $('#myForm_login').validator().on('submit', function (e) {
                                if (e.isDefaultPrevented()) {
                                    return false;
                                } else {
                                    return login_stick_stu('myForm_login');
                                }
                                return false;
                            })
                            $('#myForm_forgot').validator().on('submit', function (e) {
                                if (e.isDefaultPrevented()) {
                                    return false;
                                } else {
                                    return send_password_stick_stu('myForm_forgot');
                                }
                                return false;
                            })
                            function toggle_form(id) {
                                $(".toggle").hide();
                                $("#" + id).show();
                            }
                            function register_stick_stu(form_id) {
                                $('#screen').css({"display": "block"});
                                var type_d = $("#modal-title-reg").html();
                                var type_val = 'Shortlist_stick';
                                var open_link;
                                if (type_d.indexOf('View Phone Number') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'Phone_Info';
                                }
                                else if (type_d.indexOf('Phone') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'Phone';
                                }
                                else if (type_d.indexOf('Register to Vote up this Review') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'Voteup';
                                }
                                else if (type_d.indexOf('Email') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'Email';
                                }
                                else if (type_d.indexOf('Download') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'Download';
                                }
                                else if (type_d.indexOf('Get Contact Info') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'Contact_Info';
                                }
                                else if (type_d.indexOf('Get Updates') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'GetUpdate';
                                }
                                else if (type_d.indexOf('College Search') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'CollegeSearch';
                                }
                                else if (type_d.indexOf('Know More') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'knowmore';
                                    open_link = $("#modal-link").html();
                                }

                                //storeInfo(type_val + 'new');
                                var x = document.getElementById(form_id);
                                var form_value = {};
                                var i;
                                for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
                                    if (x.elements[i].name == 'db_access' || x.elements[i].name == 'studyAborad') {
                                        if (document.getElementById("db_access").checked == true) {
                                            form_value['db_access'] = 'Y';
                                        } else {
                                            form_value['db_access'] = 'N';
                                        }
                                        if (document.getElementById("studyAborad").checked == true) {
                                            form_value['studyAborad'] = 'Y';
                                        } else {
                                            form_value['studyAborad'] = 'N';
                                        }
                                    }
                                    else {
                                        form_value[x.elements[i].name] = x.elements[i].value;
                                    }
                                }
                                form_value['pages'] = "/colleges/national-school-of-business-nsb-bangalore$institute_profile" + "_" + type_val;
                                delete form_value['already_reg'];
                                var full_path = "https://www.collegesearch.in";
                                var main_url = full_path + "/ajax/student_registration.php";
                                $.ajax({type: "GET", url: main_url, async: false, data: form_value, success: function (response) {
                                        if (response.search("Register Successful") != -1) {
                                            if (type_val == 'Phone') {
                                                storeInfo(type_val + 'save');
                                                window.location.reload();
                                            }
                                            else if (type_val == 'Email') {
                                                storeInfo(type_val + 'save');
                                                window.location.reload();
                                            }
                                            else if (type_val == 'Download') {
                                                storeInfo(type_val + 'save');
                                                window.location.reload();
                                            }
                                            else if (type_val == 'Voteup') {
                                                alreadyLogged = 1;
                                                $('#myModal').modal('hide');
                                                $('#screen').css({"display": "none"});
                                                VoteUp();
                                                return false;

                                            }
                                            else if (type_val == 'Contact_Info') {
                                                storeInfo(type_val + 'Contact');
                                                window.open("https://www.collegesearch.in/colleges/national-school-of-business-nsb-bangalore/contact", "_self");
                                            }
                                            else if (type_val == 'Phone_Info') {
                                                storeInfo(type_val + 'Contact');
                                                //alert('Thank You for sharing the details! College will contact you soon!');
                                                window.open("https://www.collegesearch.in/colleges/national-school-of-business-nsb-bangalore/contact", "_self");
                                            }
                                            else if (type_val == 'GetUpdate') {
                                                exam_follow();
                                                storeInfo(type_val + 'GetUpdate');
                                                window.location.reload();
                                            }
                                            else if (type_val == 'knowmore') {
                                                var win = window.open(open_link, '_blank');
                                                storeInfo(type_val + '_barter');
                                                window.location.reload();
                                                win.focus();
                                            }
                                            else if (type_val == 'CollegeSearch') {
                                                storeInfo(type_val + 'CollegeSearch');
                                                window.location.reload();
                                            }
                                            else {
                                                addToShortList();
                                                storeInfo(type_val + 'Shortlist_stick');
                                                $('.select_shortlist').hide();
                                                window.location.reload();
                                            }
                                        }
                                        else {
                                            $('#screen').css({"display": "none"});
                                            alert('This Email ID already Exists. Please Login!');
                                            return false;
                                        }
                                    },
                                    error: function () {
                                        $('#screen').css({"display": "none"});
                                        return false;
                                    }
                                });
                                return false;
                            }
                            function checkDuplicateStudent_email(email) {
                                var full_path = "https://www.collegesearch.in";
                                var main_url = full_path + "/ajax.php?action=checkDuplicateStudent&email=" + email;
                                $.ajax({type: "GET", url: main_url, async: false,
                                    success: function (response) {
                                        if (response.search('Duplicate exist') != -1) {
                                            document.getElementById('email').value = '';
                                            document.getElementById('email').focus();
                                            $("#email_check").toggleClass("has-error");
                                            $("#email_check_not").toggleClass("glyphicon-remove");
                                            alert("Entered email already exists");
                                        }
                                    }
                                });
                            }
                            function login_stick_stu(form_id) {
                                $('#screen').css({"display": "block"});
                                var type_d = $("#modal-title-reg").html();
                                var type_val = 'Shortlist_stick';
                                var open_link;

                                if (type_d.indexOf('View Phone Number') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'Phone_Info';
                                }
                                else if (type_d.indexOf('Phone') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'Phone';
                                }
                                else if (type_d.indexOf('Register to Vote up this Review') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'Voteup';
                                }
                                else if (type_d.indexOf('Email') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'Email';
                                }
                                else if (type_d.indexOf('Download') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'Download';
                                }
                                else if (type_d.indexOf('Get Contact Info') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'Contact_Info';
                                }
                                else if (type_d.indexOf('Get Updates') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'GetUpdate';
                                }
                                else if (type_d.indexOf('College Search') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'CollegeSearch';
                                }
                                else if (type_d.indexOf('Know More') > -1) {
                                    type_val = 'knowmore';
                                    open_link = $("#modal-link").html();
                                }

                                //storeInfo(type_val + 'new');
                                var x = document.getElementById(form_id);
                                var form_value = {};
                                var i;
                                for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
                                    form_value[x.elements[i].name] = x.elements[i].value;
                                }
                                form_value['pages'] = "/colleges/national-school-of-business-nsb-bangalore$institute_profile" + "_" + type_val;
                                form_value['remember_student'] = 'Y';
                                var full_path = "https://www.collegesearch.in";
                                var main_url = full_path + "/ajax/student_login.php";
                                $.ajax({type: "GET", url: main_url, async: false, data: form_value, success: function (response) {
                                        if (response.search("Login Successful") != -1) {
                                            if (type_val == 'Phone') {
                                                storeInfo(type_val + 'save');
                                                window.location.reload();
                                            }
                                            else if (type_val == 'Email') {
                                                storeInfo(type_val + 'save');
                                                window.location.reload();
                                            }
                                            else if (type_val == 'Download') {
                                                storeInfo(type_val + 'save');
                                                window.location.reload();
                                            }
                                            else if (type_val == 'Contact_Info') {
                                                storeInfo(type_val + 'Contact');
                                                window.open("https://www.collegesearch.in/colleges/national-school-of-business-nsb-bangalore/contact", "_self");
                                            }
                                            else if (type_val == 'CollegeSearch') {
                                                storeInfo(type_val + 'CollegeSearch');
                                                window.location.reload();
                                            }
                                            else if (type_val == 'Voteup') {
                                                alreadyLogged = 1;
                                                $('#myModal').modal('hide');
                                                $('#screen').css({"display": "none"});
                                                VoteUp();
                                                return false;

                                            }
                                            else if (type_val == 'Phone_Info') {
                                                storeInfo(type_val + 'Contact');
                                                //alert('Thank You for sharing the details! College will contact you soon!');
                                                window.open("https://www.collegesearch.in/colleges/national-school-of-business-nsb-bangalore/contact", "_self");
                                            }
                                            else if (type_val == 'GetUpdate') {
                                                exam_follow();
                                                storeInfo(type_val + 'GetUpdate');
                                                window.location.reload();
                                            }
                                            else if (type_val == 'knowmore') {
                                                var win = window.open(open_link, '_blank');
                                                storeInfo(type_val + '_barter');
                                                window.location.reload();
                                                win.focus();
                                            }
                                            else {
                                                addToShortList();
                                                storeInfo(type_val + 'Shortlist_stick');
                                                $('.select_shortlist').hide();
                                                window.location.reload();
                                            }
                                        }
                                        else {
                                            $('#screen').css({"display": "none"});
                                            alert('Incorrect Password');
                                            return false;
                                        }
                                    },
                                    error: function () {
                                        $('#screen').css({"display": "none"});
                                        alert('Incorrect Password');
                                        return false;
                                    }
                                });
                                return false;
                            }
                            function send_password_stick_stu(form_id) {
                                var x = document.getElementById(form_id);
                                var form_value = {};
                                var i;
                                for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
                                    form_value[x.elements[i].name] = x.elements[i].value;
                                }
                                $.ajax({
                                    type: "POST",
                                    url: "https://www.collegesearch.in/ajax/ajax_forgot_password.php",
                                    data: form_value,
                                    cache: false,
                                    success: function (response)
                                    {
                                        if (response.search('success') != -1) {
                                            $("#sent_pass_error").hide();
                                            $("#sent_pass").show();
                                        } else {
                                            $("#sent_pass").hide();
                                            $("#sent_pass_error").show();
                                        }
                                    }
                                });
                                return false;
                            }

        $.ajax({type: "GET", url: main_url, async: false, success:

    }
    $('#myModal').on('show.bs.modal', function (event) {
        var button = $(event.relatedTarget) // Button that triggered the modal
        var text = button.data('head') // Extract info from data-* attributes
        // If necessary, you could initiate an AJAX request here (and then do the updating in a callback).
        // Update the modal's content. We'll use jQuery here, but you could use a data binding library or other methods instead.
        var modal = $(this)
        if(text=='College Search'){
            modal.find('#modal-title-reg').text('Register on  ' + text)
            modal.find('#modal-title-log').text('Login on  ' + text)
        }
        else{
            modal.find('#modal-title-reg').text('Register to  ' + text)
            modal.find('#modal-title-log').text('Login to  ' + text)
        }
        if (text == 'Know More') {
            var link = button.data('whatever')
            modal.find('#modal-link').text(link)
        }
    })

    function voteUpReview(id){

    main_url_fetch = "https://www.collegesearch.in/ajax/vote-up-review-bharat.php?review_id="+id;
    $.ajax({
            type: "GET",
            url: main_url_fetch,
            async: false,
            success: function (data)
            {
                if(data.search("already") > -1) {
                    alert('You have already voted up this Review.');
                }else{
                    $('#vote_up_count_'+id).html(data);
                }
                $('#vote_up_count_'+id).css('visibility','visible');
                $('#vote_up_count_'+id).prev('.helpfullBtn').prop('onclick',null);
                $('#vote_up_count_'+id).prev('.helpfullBtn').css('cursor','text');
                $('#vote_up_count_'+id).prev('.helpfullBtn').find('i.fa.fa-thumbs-up.thumbs-up-counter').css('color','#a5c82d');

            }
        });
}

function validatePhone(phone) {var pattern2 = new RegExp(/^[0]?[789]\d{9}$/);return pattern2.test(phone);}

function sendapplink(type, page) {var phone_value = $('#app_link_phone').val();
			if (phone_value.length < 10) {
                alert('Enter Valid Phone Number');return false;
            } else {
                var phone_test = validatePhone(phone_value);
                if (phone_test) {
                    if (phone_value != '') {
                        alert('SMS sent. Happy Searching!');
                        trackLinkSend('phone', phone_value, 'MobileAppPage');
                    }
                } else {
                    alert('Enter Valid Phone Numbers');
                }
        }
    }
function trackLinkSend(type, val, page) {var main_url = "https://www.collegesearch.in/ajax/track-send-mobileapp-link?type=" + type + "&val=" + val + "&page=" + page;
        $.ajax({type: "GET", url: main_url, async: false, success: function(){}
        });
    }

function selectCourse(id, course_type){
    $('#showLoad').css({"display": "block"});$('html, body').css({'overflow': 'hidden','height': '100%'});
    var dataString = 'id=' + id + '&course_type=' + course_type;
    $.ajax({ type: "POST",url: "https://www.collegesearch.in/ajax/changeCourse.php",data: dataString,cache: false,async:true,success: function (html){ window.location.href = 'https://www.collegesearch.in/colleges/national-school-of-business-nsb-bangalore'; }});
}

        function getCutoff() {
